<b>  --  Robert Pike

********************************************************************

</b>  --   (born 1956) is a Canadian 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Programmer" title="Programmer">  --  programmer

********************************************************************

</a>  --   and 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Author" title="Author">  --  author

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

<h2>  --  Life and works

********************************************************************

<a href="/w/index.php?title=Rob_Pike&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Life and works">  --  edit

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ]

********************************************************************

</h2>  --  


********************************************************************

<p>  --  He is best known for his work on the 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Go_(programming_language)" title="Go (programming language)">  --  Go programming language

********************************************************************

</a>  --   and at 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Bell_Labs" title="Bell Labs">  --  Bell Labs

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , where he was a member of the 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Unix" title="Unix">  --  Unix

********************************************************************

</a>  --   team and was involved in the creation of the 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Plan_9_from_Bell_Labs" title="Plan 9 from Bell Labs">  --  Plan 9 from Bell Labs

********************************************************************

</a>  --   and 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Inferno_(operating_system)" title="Inferno (operating system)">  --  Inferno

********************************************************************

</a>  --   operating systems, as well as the 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Limbo_programming_language" class="mw-redirect" title="Limbo programming language">  --  Limbo programming language

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .


********************************************************************

<p>  --  He also co-developed the 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Blit_(computer_terminal)" title="Blit (computer terminal)">  --  Blit

********************************************************************

</a>  --   graphical terminal for Unix; before that he wrote the first window system for Unix in 1981. Pike is the sole inventor named in US patent 4,555,775.

********************************************************************

<a href="#cite_note-1">  --  [1]

********************************************************************

</a>  --  


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Over the years Pike has written many text editors; 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Sam_(text_editor)" title="Sam (text editor)">  --  sam

********************************************************************

<a href="#cite_note-reader-2">  --  [2]

********************************************************************

</a>  --   and 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Acme_(text_editor)" title="Acme (text editor)">  --  acme

********************************************************************

</a>  --   are the most well known and are still in active use and development.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Pike, with 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Brian_Kernighan" title="Brian Kernighan">  --  Brian Kernighan

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , is the co-author of 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/The_Practice_of_Programming" title="The Practice of Programming">  --  The Practice of Programming

********************************************************************

</i>  --   and 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/The_Unix_Programming_Environment_(book)" class="mw-redirect" title="The Unix Programming Environment (book)">  --  The Unix Programming Environment

********************************************************************

</i>  --  . With 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Ken_Thompson" title="Ken Thompson">  --  Ken Thompson

********************************************************************

</a>  --   he is the co-creator of 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/UTF-8" title="UTF-8">  --  UTF-8

********************************************************************

</a>  --  . Pike also developed lesser systems such as the 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Vismon" title="Vismon">  --  vismon

********************************************************************

</a>  --   program for displaying faces of email authors.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Pike also appeared once on 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Late_Night_with_David_Letterman" title="Late Night with David Letterman">  --  Late Night with David Letterman

********************************************************************

</i>  --  , as a technical assistant to the comedy duo 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Penn_%26_Teller" title="Penn &amp; Teller">  --  Penn & Teller

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Pike worked at 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Google" title="Google">  --  Google

********************************************************************

</a>  --   from 2002 to 2021 when he retired.

********************************************************************

<a href="#cite_note-3">  --  [3]

********************************************************************

</a>  --   While at Google, he has been involved in the creation of the programming languages  

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Go_(programming_language)" title="Go (programming language)">  --  Go

********************************************************************

</a>  --   and 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Sawzall_(programming_language)" title="Sawzall (programming language)">  --  Sawzall

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="#cite_note-4">  --  [4]

********************************************************************

</a>  --   


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Pike is married to author and illustrator 

********************************************************************

<a href="/wiki/Ren%C3%A9e_French" title="Renée French">  --  Renée French

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ; the couple live in both the US and Australia.

********************************************************************

<a href="#cite_note-wowxwow-5">  --  [5]

********************************************************************

</a>  --  


********************************************************************

</p>  --  


********************************************************************
