*******************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func ServeFile(w 

********************************************************************

<a href="#ResponseWriter">  --  ResponseWriter

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , r *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , name 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  ServeFile replies to the request with the contents of the named
file or directory.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  If the provided file or directory name is a relative path, it is
interpreted relative to the current directory and may ascend to
parent directories. If the provided name is constructed from user
input, it should be sanitized before calling ServeFile.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  As a precaution, ServeFile will reject requests where r.URL.Path
contains a ".." path element; this protects against callers who
might unsafely use filepath.Join on r.URL.Path without sanitizing
it and then use that filepath.Join result as the name argument.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  As another special case, ServeFile redirects any request where r.URL.Path
ends in "/index.html" to the same path, without the final
"index.html". To avoid such redirects either modify the path or
use ServeContent.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Outside of those two special cases, ServeFile does not use
r.URL.Path for selecting the file or directory to serve; only the
file or directory provided in the name argument is used.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

        

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="ServeTLS" data-kind="function" class="Documentation-functionHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=2596">  --  ServeTLS

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#ServeTLS">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func ServeTLS(l 

********************************************************************

<a href="/net?GOOS=linux">  --  net

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/net?GOOS=linux#Listener">  --  Listener

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , handler 

********************************************************************

<a href="#Handler">  --  Handler

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , certFile, keyFile 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  ServeTLS accepts incoming HTTPS connections on the listener l,
creating a new service goroutine for each. The service goroutines
read requests and then call handler to reply to them.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  The handler is typically nil, in which case the DefaultServeMux is used.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Additionally, files containing a certificate and matching private key
for the server must be provided. If the certificate is signed by a
certificate authority, the certFile should be the concatenation
of the server's certificate, any intermediates, and the CA's certificate.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  ServeTLS always returns a non-nil error.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

        

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="SetCookie" data-kind="function" class="Documentation-functionHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/cookie.go;l=169">  --  SetCookie

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#SetCookie">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func SetCookie(w 

********************************************************************

<a href="#ResponseWriter">  --  ResponseWriter

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , cookie *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Cookie">  --  Cookie

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  SetCookie adds a Set-Cookie header to the provided ResponseWriter's headers.
The provided cookie must have a valid Name. Invalid cookies may be
silently dropped.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

        

********************************************************************

<p>  --  StatusText returns a text for the HTTP status code. It returns the empty
string if the code is unknown.

<h3 tabindex="-1" id="pkg-types" class="Documentation-typesHeader">  --  Types 

********************************************************************

<a href="#pkg-types">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</h3>  --  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Client" data-kind="type" class="Documentation-typeHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/client.go;l=58">  --  Client

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Client">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  type Client struct {


********************************************************************

<a href="#RoundTripper">  --  RoundTripper

********************************************************************

</a>  --  



********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , via []*

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</a>  --  



********************************************************************

<a href="#CookieJar">  --  CookieJar

********************************************************************

</a>  --  



********************************************************************

<a href="/time?GOOS=linux">  --  time

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/time?GOOS=linux#Duration">  --  Duration

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
}

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  A Client is an HTTP client. Its zero value (DefaultClient) is a
usable client that uses DefaultTransport.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  The Client's Transport typically has internal state (cached TCP
connections), so Clients should be reused instead of created as
needed. Clients are safe for concurrent use by multiple goroutines.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  A Client is higher-level than a RoundTripper (such as Transport)
and additionally handles HTTP details such as cookies and
redirects.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  When following redirects, the Client will forward all headers set on the
initial Request except:


********************************************************************

<p>  --  • when forwarding sensitive headers like "Authorization",
"WWW-Authenticate", and "Cookie" to untrusted targets.
These headers will be ignored when following a redirect to a domain
that is not a subdomain match or exact match of the initial domain.
For example, a redirect from "foo.com" to either "foo.com" or "sub.foo.com"
will forward the sensitive headers, but a redirect to "bar.com" will not.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  • when forwarding the "Cookie" header with a non-nil cookie Jar.
Since each redirect may mutate the state of the cookie jar,
a redirect may possibly alter a cookie set in the initial request.
When forwarding the "Cookie" header, any mutated cookies will be omitted,
with the expectation that the Jar will insert those mutated cookies
with the updated values (assuming the origin matches).
If Jar is nil, the initial cookies are forwarded without change.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  


********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Client.CloseIdleConnections" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/client.go;l=935">  --  CloseIdleConnections

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Client.CloseIdleConnections">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (c *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Client">  --  Client

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) CloseIdleConnections()

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  CloseIdleConnections closes any connections on its Transport which
were previously connected from previous requests but are now
sitting idle in a "keep-alive" state. It does not interrupt any
connections currently in use.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  If the Client's Transport does not have a CloseIdleConnections method
then this method does nothing.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Client.Do" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/client.go;l=581">  --  Do

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Client.Do">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (c *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Client">  --  Client

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) Do(req *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) (*

********************************************************************

<a href="#Response">  --  Response

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  Do sends an HTTP request and returns an HTTP response, following
policy (such as redirects, cookies, auth) as configured on the
client.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  An error is returned if caused by client policy (such as
CheckRedirect), or failure to speak HTTP (such as a network
connectivity problem). A non-2xx status code doesn't cause an
error.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  If the returned error is nil, the Response will contain a non-nil
Body which the user is expected to close. If the Body is not both
read to EOF and closed, the Client's underlying RoundTripper
(typically Transport) may not be able to re-use a persistent TCP
connection to the server for a subsequent "keep-alive" request.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  The request Body, if non-nil, will be closed by the underlying
Transport, even on errors.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  On error, any Response can be ignored. A non-nil Response with a
non-nil error only occurs when CheckRedirect fails, and even then
the returned Response.Body is already closed.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Generally Get, Post, or PostForm will be used instead of Do.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  If the server replies with a redirect, the Client first uses the
CheckRedirect function to determine whether the redirect should be
followed. If permitted, a 301, 302, or 303 redirect causes
subsequent requests to use HTTP method GET
(or HEAD if the original request was HEAD), with no body.
A 307 or 308 redirect preserves the original HTTP method and body,
provided that the Request.GetBody function is defined.
The NewRequest function automatically sets GetBody for common
standard library body types.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Any returned error will be of type *url.Error. The url.Error
value's Timeout method will report true if the request timed out.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Client.Get" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/client.go;l=475">  --  Get

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Client.Get">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (c *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Client">  --  Client

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) Get(url 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) (resp *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Response">  --  Response

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , err 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  Get issues a GET to the specified URL. If the response is one of the
following redirect codes, Get follows the redirect after calling the
Client's CheckRedirect function:


********************************************************************

<pre>  --  301 (Moved Permanently)
302 (Found)
303 (See Other)
307 (Temporary Redirect)
308 (Permanent Redirect)


********************************************************************

<p>  --  An error is returned if the Client's CheckRedirect function fails
or if there was an HTTP protocol error. A non-2xx response doesn't
cause an error. Any returned error will be of type *url.Error. The
url.Error value's Timeout method will report true if the request
timed out.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  When err is nil, resp always contains a non-nil resp.Body.
Caller should close resp.Body when done reading from it.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  To make a request with custom headers, use NewRequest and Client.Do.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  To make a request with a specified context.Context, use NewRequestWithContext
and Client.Do.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Client.Head" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/client.go;l=920">  --  Head

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Client.Head">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (c *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Client">  --  Client

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) Head(url 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) (resp *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Response">  --  Response

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , err 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  Head issues a HEAD to the specified URL. If the response is one of the
following redirect codes, Head follows the redirect after calling the
Client's CheckRedirect function:


********************************************************************

<pre>  --  301 (Moved Permanently)
302 (Found)
303 (See Other)
307 (Temporary Redirect)
308 (Permanent Redirect)


********************************************************************

<p>  --  To make a request with a specified context.Context, use NewRequestWithContext
and Client.Do.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Client.Post" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/client.go;l=843">  --  Post

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Client.Post">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (c *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Client">  --  Client

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) Post(url, contentType 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , body 

********************************************************************

<a href="/io?GOOS=linux">  --  io

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/io?GOOS=linux#Reader">  --  Reader

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) (resp *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Response">  --  Response

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , err 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  Post issues a POST to the specified URL.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Caller should close resp.Body when done reading from it.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  If the provided body is an io.Closer, it is closed after the
request.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  To set custom headers, use NewRequest and Client.Do.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  To make a request with a specified context.Context, use NewRequestWithContext
and Client.Do.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  See the Client.Do method documentation for details on how redirects
are handled.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Client.PostForm" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/client.go;l=886">  --  PostForm

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Client.PostForm">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (c *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Client">  --  Client

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) PostForm(url 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , data 

********************************************************************

<a href="/net/url?GOOS=linux">  --  url

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/net/url?GOOS=linux#Values">  --  Values

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) (resp *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Response">  --  Response

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , err 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  PostForm issues a POST to the specified URL,
with data's keys and values URL-encoded as the request body.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  The Content-Type header is set to application/x-www-form-urlencoded.
To set other headers, use NewRequest and Client.Do.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  When err is nil, resp always contains a non-nil resp.Body.
Caller should close resp.Body when done reading from it.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  See the Client.Do method documentation for details on how redirects
are handled.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  To make a request with a specified context.Context, use NewRequestWithContext
and Client.Do.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="CloseNotifier" data-kind="type" class="Documentation-typeHeader">  --  
          

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=216">  --  CloseNotifier

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
            

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

      

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  type CloseNotifier interface {


********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#bool">  --  bool

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
}

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  The CloseNotifier interface is implemented by ResponseWriters which
allow detecting when the underlying connection has gone away.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  This mechanism can be used to cancel long operations on the server
if the client has disconnected before the response is ready.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Deprecated: the CloseNotifier interface predates Go's context package.
New code should use Request.Context instead.


********************************************************************

</p>  --

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Dir" data-kind="type" class="Documentation-typeHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/fs.go;l=44">  --  Dir

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Dir">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  type Dir 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  A Dir implements FileSystem using the native file system restricted to a
specific directory tree.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  While the FileSystem.Open method takes '/'-separated paths, a Dir's string
value is a filename on the native file system, not a URL, so it is separated
by filepath.Separator, which isn't necessarily '/'.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Note that Dir could expose sensitive files and directories. Dir will follow
symlinks pointing out of the directory tree, which can be especially dangerous
if serving from a directory in which users are able to create arbitrary symlinks.
Dir will also allow access to files and directories starting with a period,
which could expose sensitive directories like .git or sensitive files like
.htpasswd. To exclude files with a leading period, remove the files/directories
from the server or create a custom FileSystem implementation.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  An empty Dir is treated as ".".


********************************************************************

</p>  --  


********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Dir.Open" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="FileSystem" data-kind="type" class="Documentation-typeHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/fs.go;l=96">  --  FileSystem

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#FileSystem">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  type FileSystem interface {


********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) (

********************************************************************

<a href="#File">  --  File

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )


********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  A FileSystem implements access to a collection of named files.
The elements in a file path are separated by slash ('/', U+002F)
characters, regardless of host operating system convention.
See the FileServer function to convert a FileSystem to a Handler.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  This interface predates the fs.FS interface, which can be used instead:
the FS adapter function converts an fs.FS to a FileSystem.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  


********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func FS(fsys 

********************************************************************

<a href="/io/fs?GOOS=linux">  --  fs

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/io/fs?GOOS=linux#FS">  --  FS

<p>  --  FS converts fsys to a FileSystem implementation,

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Flusher" data-kind="type" class="Documentation-typeHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=173">  --  Flusher

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Flusher">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  type Flusher interface {


********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  The Flusher interface is implemented by ResponseWriters that allow
an HTTP handler to flush buffered data to the client.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  The default HTTP/1.x and HTTP/2 ResponseWriter implementations
support Flusher, but ResponseWriter wrappers may not. Handlers
should always test for this ability at runtime.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Note that even for ResponseWriters that support Flush,
if the client is connected through an HTTP proxy,
the buffered data may not reach the client until the response
completes.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

    

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Handler" data-kind="type" class="Documentation-typeHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=86">  --  Handler

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Handler">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  type Handler interface {


********************************************************************

<a href="#ResponseWriter">  --  ResponseWriter

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )


********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  A Handler responds to an HTTP request.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  ServeHTTP should write reply headers and data to the ResponseWriter
and then return. Returning signals that the request is finished; it
is not valid to use the ResponseWriter or read from the
Request.Body after or concurrently with the completion of the
ServeHTTP call.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Depending on the HTTP client software, HTTP protocol version, and
any intermediaries between the client and the Go server, it may not
be possible to read from the Request.Body after writing to the
ResponseWriter. Cautious handlers should read the Request.Body
first, and then reply.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Except for reading the body, handlers should not modify the
provided Request.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  If ServeHTTP panics, the server (the caller of ServeHTTP) assumes
that the effect of the panic was isolated to the active request.
It recovers the panic, logs a stack trace to the server error log,
and either closes the network connection or sends an HTTP/2
RST_STREAM, depending on the HTTP protocol. To abort a handler so
the client sees an interrupted response but the server doesn't log
an error, panic with the value ErrAbortHandler.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  


********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="AllowQuerySemicolons" data-kind="function" class="Documentation-typeFuncHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=2950">  --  AllowQuerySemicolons

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#AllowQuerySemicolons">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func AllowQuerySemicolons(h 

********************************************************************

<a href="#Handler">  --  Handler

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) 

********************************************************************

<a href="#Handler">  --  Handler

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  AllowQuerySemicolons returns a handler that serves requests by converting any
unescaped semicolons in the URL query to ampersands, and invoking the handler h.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  This restores the pre-Go 1.17 behavior of splitting query parameters on both
semicolons and ampersands. (See golang.org/issue/25192). Note that this
behavior doesn't match that of many proxies, and the mismatch can lead to
security issues.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  AllowQuerySemicolons should be invoked before Request.ParseForm is called.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="FileServer" data-kind="function" class="Documentation-typeFuncHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/fs.go;l=856">  --  FileServer

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#FileServer">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func FileServer(root 

********************************************************************

<a href="#FileSystem">  --  FileSystem

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) 

********************************************************************

<a href="#Handler">  --  Handler

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  FileServer returns a handler that serves HTTP requests
with the contents of the file system rooted at root.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  As a special case, the returned file server redirects any request
ending in "/index.html" to the same path, without the final
"index.html".


********************************************************************

<p>  --  To use the operating system's file system implementation,
use http.Dir:


********************************************************************

<pre>  --  http.Handle("/", http.FileServer(http.Dir("/tmp")))


********************************************************************

<p>  --  To use an fs.FS implementation, use http.FS to convert it:


********************************************************************

<pre>  --  http.Handle("/", http.FileServer(http.FS(fsys)))


********************************************************************

</pre>  --  


********************************************************************

<a href="#example-FileServer">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  


********************************************************************

<pre class="Documentation-exampleCode">  --  
package main

import (
	"log"
	"net/http"
)

func main() {
	// Simple static webserver:
	log.Fatal(http.ListenAndServe(":8080", http.FileServer(http.Dir("/usr/share/doc"))))
}


********************************************************************

</pre>  --  



********************************************************************

<pre>  --  Output:

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  


********************************************************************

</p>  --  
        

********************************************************************

<a href="#example-FileServer-DotFileHiding">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  


********************************************************************

<pre class="Documentation-exampleCode">  --  
package main

import (
	"io/fs"
	"log"
	"net/http"
	"strings"
)

// containsDotFile reports whether name contains a path element starting with a period.
// The name is assumed to be a delimited by forward slashes, as guaranteed
// by the http.FileSystem interface.
func containsDotFile(name string) bool {
	parts := strings.Split(name, "/")
	for _, part := range parts {
		if strings.HasPrefix(part, ".") {
			return true
		}
	}
	return false
}

// dotFileHidingFile is the http.File use in dotFileHidingFileSystem.
// It is used to wrap the Readdir method of http.File so that we can
// remove files and directories that start with a period from its output.
type dotFileHidingFile struct {
	http.File
}

// Readdir is a wrapper around the Readdir method of the embedded File
// that filters out all files that start with a period in their name.
func (f dotFileHidingFile) Readdir(n int) (fis []fs.FileInfo, err error) {
	files, err := f.File.Readdir(n)
	for _, file := range files { // Filters out the dot files
		if !strings.HasPrefix(file.Name(), ".") {
			fis = append(fis, file)
		}
	}
	return
}

// dotFileHidingFileSystem is an http.FileSystem that hides
// hidden "dot files" from being served.
type dotFileHidingFileSystem struct {
	http.FileSystem
}

// Open is a wrapper around the Open method of the embedded FileSystem
// that serves a 403 permission error when name has a file or directory
// with whose name starts with a period in its path.
func (fsys dotFileHidingFileSystem) Open(name string) (http.File, error) {
	if containsDotFile(name) { // If dot file, return 403 response
		return nil, fs.ErrPermission
	}

	file, err := fsys.FileSystem.Open(name)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	return dotFileHidingFile{file}, err
}

func main() {
	fsys := dotFileHidingFileSystem{http.Dir(".")}
	http.Handle("/", http.FileServer(fsys))
	log.Fatal(http.ListenAndServe(":8080", nil))
}


********************************************************************

</pre>  --  



********************************************************************

<pre>  --  Output:

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  


********************************************************************

</p>  --  
        

********************************************************************

<a href="#example-FileServer-StripPrefix">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  


********************************************************************

<pre class="Documentation-exampleCode">  --

	"net/http"
)

	// To serve a directory on disk (/tmp) under an alternate URL
	// path (/tmpfiles/), use StripPrefix to modify the request
	// URL's path before the FileServer sees it:
	http.Handle("/tmpfiles/", http.StripPrefix("/tmpfiles/", http.FileServer(http.Dir("/tmp"))))

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="NotFoundHandler" data-kind="function" class="Documentation-typeFuncHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=2143">  --  NotFoundHandler

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#NotFoundHandler">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func NotFoundHandler() 

********************************************************************

<a href="#Handler">  --  Handler

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  NotFoundHandler returns a simple request handler
that replies to each request with a “404 page not found” reply.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  


********************************************************************

<a href="#example-NotFoundHandler">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  


********************************************************************

<pre class="Documentation-exampleCode">  --  
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"net/http"
)

func newPeopleHandler() http.Handler {
	return http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
		fmt.Fprintln(w, "This is the people handler.")
	})
}

func main() {
	mux := http.NewServeMux()

	// Create sample handler to returns 404
	mux.Handle("/resources", http.NotFoundHandler())

	// Create sample handler that returns 200
	mux.Handle("/resources/people/", newPeopleHandler())

	log.Fatal(http.ListenAndServe(":8080", mux))
}

</pre>  --

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="StripPrefix" data-kind="function" class="Documentation-typeFuncHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=2151">  --  StripPrefix

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#StripPrefix">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func StripPrefix(prefix 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , h 

********************************************************************

<a href="#Handler">  --  Handler

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) 

********************************************************************

<a href="#Handler">  --  Handler

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  StripPrefix returns a handler that serves HTTP requests by removing the
given prefix from the request URL's Path (and RawPath if set) and invoking
the handler h. StripPrefix handles a request for a path that doesn't begin
with prefix by replying with an HTTP 404 not found error. The prefix must
match exactly: if the prefix in the request contains escaped characters
the reply is also an HTTP 404 not found error.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  


********************************************************************

<a href="#example-StripPrefix">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  


********************************************************************

<pre class="Documentation-exampleCode">  --  
package main

import (
	"net/http"
)

func main() {
	// To serve a directory on disk (/tmp) under an alternate URL
	// path (/tmpfiles/), use StripPrefix to modify the request
	// URL's path before the FileServer sees it:
	http.Handle("/tmpfiles/", http.StripPrefix("/tmpfiles/", http.FileServer(http.Dir("/tmp"))))
}

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="TimeoutHandler" data-kind="function" class="Documentation-typeFuncHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=3346">  --  TimeoutHandler

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#TimeoutHandler">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func TimeoutHandler(h 

********************************************************************

<a href="#Handler">  --  Handler

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , dt 

********************************************************************

<a href="/time?GOOS=linux">  --  time

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/time?GOOS=linux#Duration">  --  Duration

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , msg 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) 

********************************************************************

<a href="#Handler">  --  Handler

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  TimeoutHandler returns a Handler that runs h with the given time limit.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  The new Handler calls h.ServeHTTP to handle each request, but if a
call runs for longer than its time limit, the handler responds with
a 503 Service Unavailable error and the given message in its body.
(If msg is empty, a suitable default message will be sent.)
After such a timeout, writes by h to its ResponseWriter will return
ErrHandlerTimeout.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  TimeoutHandler supports the Pusher interface but does not support
the Hijacker or Flusher interfaces.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Hijacker" data-kind="type" class="Documentation-typeHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=185">  --  Hijacker

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Hijacker">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  type Hijacker interface {


********************************************************************

<a href="/net?GOOS=linux">  --  net

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/net?GOOS=linux#Conn">  --  Conn

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , *

********************************************************************

<a href="/bufio?GOOS=linux">  --  bufio

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/bufio?GOOS=linux#ReadWriter">  --  ReadWriter

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )
}

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  The Hijacker interface is implemented by ResponseWriters that allow
an HTTP handler to take over the connection.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  The default ResponseWriter for HTTP/1.x connections supports
Hijacker, but HTTP/2 connections intentionally do not.
ResponseWriter wrappers may also not support Hijacker. Handlers
should always test for this ability at runtime.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  


********************************************************************

<a href="#example-Hijacker">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  


********************************************************************

<pre class="Documentation-exampleCode">  --  
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"net/http"
)

func main() {
	http.HandleFunc("/hijack", func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
		hj, ok := w.(http.Hijacker)
		if !ok {
			http.Error(w, "webserver doesn't support hijacking", http.StatusInternalServerError)
			return
		}
		conn, bufrw, err := hj.Hijack()
		if err != nil {
			http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)
			return
		}
		// Don't forget to close the connection:
		defer conn.Close()
		bufrw.WriteString("Now we're speaking raw TCP. Say hi: ")
		bufrw.Flush()
		s, err := bufrw.ReadString('\n')
		if err != nil {
			log.Printf("error reading string: %v", err)
			return
		}
		fmt.Fprintf(bufrw, "You said: %q\nBye.\n", s)
		bufrw.Flush()
	})
}


********************************************************************

</pre>  --  



********************************************************************

<pre>  --  Output:

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  


********************************************************************

</p>  --  
        

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="MaxBytesError" data-kind="type" class="Documentation-typeHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/request.go;l=1122">  --  MaxBytesError

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#MaxBytesError">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  type MaxBytesError struct {


********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#int64">  --  int64

********************************************************************

</a>  --  


********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="NewRequestWithContext" data-kind="function" class="Documentation-typeFuncHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/request.go;l=838">  --  NewRequestWithContext

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#NewRequestWithContext">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func NewRequestWithContext(ctx 

********************************************************************

<a href="/context?GOOS=linux">  --  context

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/context?GOOS=linux#Context">  --  Context

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , method, url 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , body 

********************************************************************

<a href="/io?GOOS=linux">  --  io

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/io?GOOS=linux#Reader">  --  Reader

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) (*

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  NewRequestWithContext returns a new Request given a method, URL, and
optional body.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  If the provided body is also an io.Closer, the returned
Request.Body is set to body and will be closed by the Client
methods Do, Post, and PostForm, and Transport.RoundTrip.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  NewRequestWithContext returns a Request suitable for use with
Client.Do or Transport.RoundTrip. To create a request for use with
testing a Server Handler, either use the NewRequest function in the
net/http/httptest package, use ReadRequest, or manually update the
Request fields. For an outgoing client request, the context
controls the entire lifetime of a request and its response:
obtaining a connection, sending the request, and reading the
response headers and body. See the Request type's documentation for
the difference between inbound and outbound request fields.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  If body is of type *bytes.Buffer, *bytes.Reader, or
*strings.Reader, the returned request's ContentLength is set to its
exact value (instead of -1), GetBody is populated (so 307 and 308
redirects can replay the body), and Body is set to NoBody if the
ContentLength is 0.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="ReadRequest" data-kind="function" class="Documentation-typeFuncHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/request.go;l=997">  --  ReadRequest

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#ReadRequest">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func ReadRequest(b *

********************************************************************

<a href="/bufio?GOOS=linux">  --  bufio

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/bufio?GOOS=linux#Reader">  --  Reader

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) (*

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  ReadRequest reads and parses an incoming request from b.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  ReadRequest is a low-level function and should only be used for
specialized applications; most code should use the Server to read
requests and handle them via the Handler interface. ReadRequest
only supports HTTP/1.x requests. For HTTP/2, use golang.org/x/net/http2.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Request.AddCookie" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/request.go;l=437">  --  AddCookie

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Request.AddCookie">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (r *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) AddCookie(c *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Cookie">  --  Cookie

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  AddCookie adds a cookie to the request. Per 

********************************************************************

<a href="https://rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6265.html#section-5.4">  --  RFC 6265 section 5.4

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ,
AddCookie does not attach more than one Cookie header field. That
means all cookies, if any, are written into the same line,
separated by semicolon.
AddCookie only sanitizes c's name and value, and does not sanitize
a Cookie header already present in the request.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Request.Clone" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/request.go;l=372">  --  Clone

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Request.Clone">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (r *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) Clone(ctx 

********************************************************************

<a href="/context?GOOS=linux">  --  context

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/context?GOOS=linux#Context">  --  Context

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  Clone returns a deep copy of r with its context changed to ctx.
The provided ctx must be non-nil.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  For an outgoing client request, the context controls the entire
lifetime of a request and its response: obtaining a connection,
sending the request, and reading the response headers and body.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Request.Context" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/request.go;l=340">  --  Context

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Request.Context">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (r *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) Context() 

********************************************************************

<a href="/context?GOOS=linux">  --  context

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/context?GOOS=linux#Context">  --  Context

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  Context returns the request's context. To change the context, use
Clone or WithContext.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  The returned context is always non-nil; it defaults to the
background context.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  For outgoing client requests, the context controls cancellation.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  For incoming server requests, the context is canceled when the
client's connection closes, the request is canceled (with HTTP/2),
or when the ServeHTTP method returns.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Request.Cookie" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Request.FormValue" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/request.go;l=1343">  --  FormValue

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Request.FormValue">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (r *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) FormValue(key 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  FormValue returns the first value for the named component of the query.
POST and PUT body parameters take precedence over URL query string values.
FormValue calls ParseMultipartForm and ParseForm if necessary and ignores
any errors returned by these functions.
If key is not present, FormValue returns the empty string.
To access multiple values of the same key, call ParseForm and
then inspect Request.Form directly.


********************************************************************

</p>  --

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Request.MultipartReader" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --
