</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (r *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) MultipartReader() (*

********************************************************************

<a href="/mime/multipart?GOOS=linux">  --  multipart

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/mime/multipart?GOOS=linux#Reader">  --  Reader

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  MultipartReader returns a MIME multipart reader if this is a
multipart/form-data or a multipart/mixed POST request, else returns nil and an error.
Use this function instead of ParseMultipartForm to
process the request body as a stream.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Request.ParseForm" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/request.go;l=1255">  --  ParseForm

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Request.ParseForm">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (r *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) ParseForm() 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  ParseForm populates r.Form and r.PostForm.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  For all requests, ParseForm parses the raw query from the URL and updates
r.Form.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  For POST, PUT, and PATCH requests, it also reads the request body, parses it
as a form and puts the results into both r.PostForm and r.Form. Request body
parameters take precedence over URL query string values in r.Form.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  If the request Body's size has not already been limited by MaxBytesReader,
the size is capped at 10MB.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  For other HTTP methods, or when the Content-Type is not
application/x-www-form-urlencoded, the request Body is not read, and
r.PostForm is initialized to a non-nil, empty value.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  ParseMultipartForm calls ParseForm automatically.
ParseForm is idempotent.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Request.ParseMultipartForm" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/request.go;l=1298">  --  ParseMultipartForm

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Request.ParseMultipartForm">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (r *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) ParseMultipartForm(maxMemory 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#int64">  --  int64

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  ParseMultipartForm parses a request body as multipart/form-data.
The whole request body is parsed and up to a total of maxMemory bytes of
its file parts are stored in memory, with the remainder stored on
disk in temporary files.
ParseMultipartForm calls ParseForm if necessary.
If ParseForm returns an error, ParseMultipartForm returns it but also
continues parsing the request body.
After one call to ParseMultipartForm, subsequent calls have no effect.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Request.PostFormValue" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/request.go;l=1358">  --  PostFormValue

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Request.PostFormValue">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (r *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) PostFormValue(key 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  PostFormValue returns the first value for the named component of the POST,
PATCH, or PUT request body. URL query parameters are ignored.
PostFormValue calls ParseMultipartForm and ParseForm if necessary and ignores
any errors returned by these functions.
If key is not present, PostFormValue returns the empty string.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Request.Referer" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/request.go;l=454">  --  Referer

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Request.Referer">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (r *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) Referer() 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  Referer returns the referring URL, if sent in the request.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Referer is misspelled as in the request itself, a mistake from the
earliest days of HTTP.  This value can also be fetched from the
Header map as Header["Referer"]; the benefit of making it available
as a method is that the compiler can diagnose programs that use the
alternate (correct English) spelling req.Referrer() but cannot
diagnose programs that use Header["Referrer"].


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Request.SetBasicAuth" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/request.go;l=961">  --  SetBasicAuth

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Request.SetBasicAuth">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (r *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) SetBasicAuth(username, password 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  SetBasicAuth sets the request's Authorization header to use HTTP
Basic Authentication with the provided username and password.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  With HTTP Basic Authentication the provided username and password
are not encrypted. It should generally only be used in an HTTPS
request.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  The username may not contain a colon. Some protocols may impose
additional requirements on pre-escaping the username and
password. For instance, when used with OAuth2, both arguments must
be URL encoded first with url.QueryEscape.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Request.WithContext" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/request.go;l=356">  --  WithContext

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Request.WithContext">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (r *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) WithContext(ctx 

********************************************************************

<a href="/context?GOOS=linux">  --  context

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/context?GOOS=linux#Context">  --  Context

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  WithContext returns a shallow copy of r with its context changed
to ctx. The provided ctx must be non-nil.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  For outgoing client request, the context controls the entire
lifetime of a request and its response: obtaining a connection,
sending the request, and reading the response headers and body.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  To create a new request with a context, use NewRequestWithContext.
To make a deep copy of a request with a new context, use Request.Clone.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Request.Write" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/request.go;l=534">  --  Write

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Request.Write">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (r *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) Write(w 

********************************************************************

<a href="/io?GOOS=linux">  --  io

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/io?GOOS=linux#Writer">  --  Writer

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  Write writes an HTTP/1.1 request, which is the header and body, in wire format.
This method consults the following fields of the request:


********************************************************************

<pre>  --  Host
URL
Method (defaults to "GET")
Header
ContentLength
TransferEncoding
Body


********************************************************************

<p>  --  If Body is present, Content-Length is <= 0 and TransferEncoding
hasn't been set to "identity", Write adds "Transfer-Encoding:
chunked" to the header. Body is closed after it is sent.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Request.WriteProxy" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/request.go;l=544">  --  WriteProxy

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Request.WriteProxy">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (r *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) WriteProxy(w 

********************************************************************

<a href="/io?GOOS=linux">  --  io

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/io?GOOS=linux#Writer">  --  Writer

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  WriteProxy is like Write but writes the request in the form
expected by an HTTP proxy. In particular, WriteProxy writes the
initial Request-URI line of the request with an absolute URI, per
section 5.3 of 

********************************************************************

<a href="https://rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc7230.html">  --  RFC 7230

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , including the scheme and host.
In either case, WriteProxy also writes a Host header, using
either r.Host or r.URL.Host.


********************************************************************

</p>  --

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Get" data-kind="function" class="Documentation-typeFuncHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/client.go;l=448">  --  Get

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Get">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func Get(url 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) (resp *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Response">  --  Response

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , err 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  Get issues a GET to the specified URL. If the response is one of
the following redirect codes, Get follows the redirect, up to a
maximum of 10 redirects:


********************************************************************

<pre>  --  301 (Moved Permanently)
302 (Found)
303 (See Other)
307 (Temporary Redirect)
308 (Permanent Redirect)


********************************************************************

<p>  --  An error is returned if there were too many redirects or if there
was an HTTP protocol error. A non-2xx response doesn't cause an
error. Any returned error will be of type *url.Error. The url.Error
value's Timeout method will report true if the request timed out.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  When err is nil, resp always contains a non-nil resp.Body.
Caller should close resp.Body when done reading from it.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Get is a wrapper around DefaultClient.Get.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  To make a request with custom headers, use NewRequest and
DefaultClient.Do.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  To make a request with a specified context.Context, use NewRequestWithContext
and DefaultClient.Do.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  


********************************************************************

<a href="#example-Get">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  


********************************************************************

<pre class="Documentation-exampleCode">  --  
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"io"
	"log"
	"net/http"
)

func main() {
	res, err := http.Get("http://www.google.com/robots.txt")
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatal(err)
	}
	body, err := io.ReadAll(res.Body)
	res.Body.Close()
	if res.StatusCode > 299 {
		log.Fatalf("Response failed with status code: %d and\nbody: %s\n", res.StatusCode, body)
	}
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatal(err)
	}
	fmt.Printf("%s", body)
}


********************************************************************

</pre>  --  



********************************************************************

<pre>  --  Output:

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  


********************************************************************

</p>  --  
        

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="PostForm" data-kind="function" class="Documentation-typeFuncHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/client.go;l=868">  --  PostForm

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#PostForm">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func PostForm(url 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , data 

********************************************************************

<a href="/net/url?GOOS=linux">  --  url

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/net/url?GOOS=linux#Values">  --  Values

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) (resp *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Response">  --  Response

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , err 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  PostForm issues a POST to the specified URL, with data's keys and
values URL-encoded as the request body.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  The Content-Type header is set to application/x-www-form-urlencoded.
To set other headers, use NewRequest and DefaultClient.Do.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  When err is nil, resp always contains a non-nil resp.Body.
Caller should close resp.Body when done reading from it.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  PostForm is a wrapper around DefaultClient.PostForm.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  See the Client.Do method documentation for details on how redirects
are handled.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  To make a request with a specified context.Context, use NewRequestWithContext
and DefaultClient.Do.


********************************************************************

</p>  --

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="ReadResponse" data-kind="function" class="Documentation-typeFuncHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/response.go;l=154">  --  ReadResponse

********************************************************************

</a>  --

<p>  --  ReadResponse reads and returns an HTTP response from r.
The req parameter optionally specifies the Request that corresponds
to this Response. If nil, a GET request is assumed.
Clients must call resp.Body.Close when finished reading resp.Body.
After that call, clients can inspect resp.Trailer to find key/value
pairs included in the response trailer.

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="ResponseController" data-kind="type" class="Documentation-typeHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/responsecontroller.go;l=17">  --  ResponseController

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#ResponseController">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  type ResponseController struct {
	

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  A ResponseController is used by an HTTP handler to control the response.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  A ResponseController may not be used after the Handler.ServeHTTP method has returned.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  


********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="NewResponseController" data-kind="function" class="Documentation-typeFuncHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/responsecontroller.go;l=37">  --  NewResponseController

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#NewResponseController">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func NewResponseController(rw 

********************************************************************

<a href="#ResponseWriter">  --  ResponseWriter

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) *

********************************************************************

<a href="#ResponseController">  --  ResponseController

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  NewResponseController creates a ResponseController for a request.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  The ResponseWriter should be the original value passed to the Handler.ServeHTTP method,
or have an Unwrap method returning the original ResponseWriter.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  If the ResponseWriter implements any of the following methods, the ResponseController
will call them as appropriate:


********************************************************************

<pre>  --  Flush()
FlushError() error // alternative Flush returning an error
Hijack() (net.Conn, *bufio.ReadWriter, error)
SetReadDeadline(deadline time.Time) error
SetWriteDeadline(deadline time.Time) error


********************************************************************

<p>  --  If the ResponseWriter does not support a method, ResponseController returns
an error matching ErrNotSupported.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="ResponseController.SetReadDeadline" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/responsecontroller.go;l=84">  --  SetReadDeadline

</a>  --

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#ResponseController.SetReadDeadline">  --  ¶

</a>  --

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (c *

********************************************************************

<a href="#ResponseController">  --  ResponseController

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) SetReadDeadline(deadline 

********************************************************************

<a href="/time?GOOS=linux">  --  time

<p>  --  SetReadDeadline sets the deadline for reading the entire request, including the body.
Reads from the request body after the deadline has been exceeded will return an error.
A zero value means no deadline.

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="ResponseController.SetWriteDeadline" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/responsecontroller.go;l=104">  --  SetWriteDeadline

********************************************************************

</a>  --

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#ResponseController.SetWriteDeadline">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (c *

********************************************************************

<a href="#ResponseController">  --  ResponseController

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) SetWriteDeadline(deadline 

********************************************************************

<a href="/time?GOOS=linux">  --  time

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

<a href="/time?GOOS=linux#Time">  --  Time

<p>  --  SetWriteDeadline sets the deadline for writing the response.
Writes to the response body after the deadline has been exceeded will not block,
but may succeed if the data has been buffered.
A zero value means no deadline.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Setting the write deadline after it has been exceeded will not extend it.

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="ResponseWriter" data-kind="type" class="Documentation-typeHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=95">  --  ResponseWriter

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#ResponseWriter">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  type ResponseWriter interface {


********************************************************************

<a href="#Header">  --  Header

********************************************************************

</a>  --  



********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#byte">  --  byte

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) (

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#int">  --  int

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )



********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#int">  --  int

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )
}

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  A ResponseWriter interface is used by an HTTP handler to
construct an HTTP response.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  A ResponseWriter may not be used after the Handler.ServeHTTP method
has returned.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  


********************************************************************

<a href="#example-ResponseWriter-Trailers">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  


********************************************************************

<p>  --  HTTP Trailers are a set of key/value pairs like headers that come
after the HTTP response, instead of before.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  



********************************************************************

<pre class="Documentation-exampleCode">  --  
package main

import (
	"io"
	"net/http"
)

func main() {
	mux := http.NewServeMux()
	mux.HandleFunc("/sendstrailers", func(w http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request) {
		// Before any call to WriteHeader or Write, declare
		// the trailers you will set during the HTTP
		// response. These three headers are actually sent in
		// the trailer.
		w.Header().Set("Trailer", "AtEnd1, AtEnd2")
		w.Header().Add("Trailer", "AtEnd3")

		w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "text/plain; charset=utf-8") // normal header
		w.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)

		w.Header().Set("AtEnd1", "value 1")
		io.WriteString(w, "This HTTP response has both headers before this text and trailers at the end.\n")
		w.Header().Set("AtEnd2", "value 2")
		w.Header().Set("AtEnd3", "value 3") // These will appear as trailers.
	})
}


********************************************************************

</pre>  --  



********************************************************************

<pre>  --  Output:

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  


********************************************************************

</p>  --  
        

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="RoundTripper" data-kind="type" class="Documentation-typeHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/client.go;l=117">  --  RoundTripper

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#RoundTripper">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  type RoundTripper interface {


********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) (*

********************************************************************

<a href="#Response">  --  Response

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )
}

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  RoundTripper is an interface representing the ability to execute a
single HTTP transaction, obtaining the Response for a given Request.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  A RoundTripper must be safe for concurrent use by multiple
goroutines.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  


********************************************************************

<pre>  --  var DefaultTransport 

********************************************************************

<a href="#RoundTripper">  --  RoundTripper

********************************************************************

</a>  --   = &

********************************************************************

<a href="#Transport">  --  Transport

********************************************************************

</a>  --  {


********************************************************************

<a href="#ProxyFromEnvironment">  --  ProxyFromEnvironment

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ,
	DialContext: defaultTransportDialContext(&

********************************************************************

<a href="/net?GOOS=linux">  --  net

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/net?GOOS=linux#Dialer">  --  Dialer

********************************************************************

</a>  --  {
		Timeout:   30 * 

********************************************************************

<a href="/time?GOOS=linux">  --  time

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/time?GOOS=linux#Second">  --  Second

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ,
		KeepAlive: 30 * 

********************************************************************

<a href="/time?GOOS=linux">  --  time

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/time?GOOS=linux#Second">  --  Second

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ,
	}),
	ForceAttemptHTTP2:     

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#true">  --  true

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ,
	MaxIdleConns:          100,
	IdleConnTimeout:       90 * 

********************************************************************

<a href="/time?GOOS=linux">  --  time

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/time?GOOS=linux#Second">  --  Second

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ,
	TLSHandshakeTimeout:   10 * 

********************************************************************

<a href="/time?GOOS=linux">  --  time

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/time?GOOS=linux#Second">  --  Second

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ,
	ExpectContinueTimeout: 1 * 

********************************************************************

<a href="/time?GOOS=linux">  --  time

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/time?GOOS=linux#Second">  --  Second

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ,
}

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  DefaultTransport is the default implementation of Transport and is
used by DefaultClient. It establishes network connections as needed
and caches them for reuse by subsequent calls. It uses HTTP proxies
as directed by the environment variables HTTP_PROXY, HTTPS_PROXY
and NO_PROXY (or the lowercase versions thereof).


********************************************************************

</p>  --

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="NewFileTransport" data-kind="function" class="Documentation-typeFuncHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/filetransport.go;l=30">  --  NewFileTransport

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#NewFileTransport">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func NewFileTransport(fs 

********************************************************************

<a href="#FileSystem">  --  FileSystem

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) 

********************************************************************

<a href="#RoundTripper">  --  RoundTripper

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  NewFileTransport returns a new RoundTripper, serving the provided
FileSystem. The returned RoundTripper ignores the URL host in its
incoming requests, as well as most other properties of the
request.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  The typical use case for NewFileTransport is to register the "file"
protocol with a Transport, as in:


********************************************************************

<pre>  --  t := &http.Transport{}
t.RegisterProtocol("file", http.NewFileTransport(http.Dir("/")))
c := &http.Client{Transport: t}
res, err := c.Get("file:///etc/passwd")
...


********************************************************************

</pre>  --

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="SameSite" data-kind="type" class="Documentation-typeHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/cookie.go;l=49">  --  SameSite

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#SameSite">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  type SameSite 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#int">  --  int

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  SameSite allows a server to define a cookie attribute making it impossible for
the browser to send this cookie along with cross-site requests. The main
goal is to mitigate the risk of cross-origin information leakage, and provide
some protection against cross-site request forgery attacks.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  See 

********************************************************************

<a href="https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-ietf-httpbis-cookie-same-site-00">  --  https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-ietf-httpbis-cookie-same-site-00

********************************************************************

</a>  --   for details.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  


********************************************************************

<pre>  --  const (


********************************************************************

<a href="#SameSite">  --  SameSite

********************************************************************

</a>  --   = 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#iota">  --  iota

********************************************************************

</a>  --   + 1


********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="ServeMux" data-kind="type" class="Documentation-typeHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=2306">  --  ServeMux

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#ServeMux">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  type ServeMux struct {
	

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  ServeMux is an HTTP request multiplexer.
It matches the URL of each incoming request against a list of registered
patterns and calls the handler for the pattern that
most closely matches the URL.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Patterns name fixed, rooted paths, like "/favicon.ico",
or rooted subtrees, like "/images/" (note the trailing slash).
Longer patterns take precedence over shorter ones, so that
if there are handlers registered for both "/images/"
and "/images/thumbnails/", the latter handler will be
called for paths beginning "/images/thumbnails/" and the
former will receive requests for any other paths in the
"/images/" subtree.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Note that since a pattern ending in a slash names a rooted subtree,
the pattern "/" matches all paths not matched by other registered
patterns, not just the URL with Path == "/".


********************************************************************

<p>  --  If a subtree has been registered and a request is received naming the
subtree root without its trailing slash, ServeMux redirects that
request to the subtree root (adding the trailing slash). This behavior can
be overridden with a separate registration for the path without
the trailing slash. For example, registering "/images/" causes ServeMux
to redirect a request for "/images" to "/images/", unless "/images" has
been registered separately.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Patterns may optionally begin with a host name, restricting matches to
URLs on that host only. Host-specific patterns take precedence over
general patterns, so that a handler might register for the two patterns
"/codesearch" and "codesearch.google.com/" without also taking over
requests for "

********************************************************************

<a href="http://www.google.com/">  --  http://www.google.com/

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ".


********************************************************************

<p>  --  ServeMux also takes care of sanitizing the URL request path and the Host
header, stripping the port number and redirecting any request containing . or
.. elements or repeated slashes to an equivalent, cleaner URL.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  


********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="NewServeMux" data-kind="function" class="Documentation-typeFuncHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=2319">  --  NewServeMux

********************************************************************

</a>  --

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="ServeMux.Handle" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=2505">  --  Handle

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#ServeMux.Handle">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (mux *

********************************************************************

<a href="#ServeMux">  --  ServeMux

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) Handle(pattern 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , handler 

********************************************************************

<a href="#Handler">  --  Handler

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  Handle registers the handler for the given pattern.
If a handler already exists for pattern, Handle panics.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  


********************************************************************

<a href="#example-ServeMux.Handle">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  


********************************************************************

<pre class="Documentation-exampleCode">  --  
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"net/http"
)

type apiHandler struct{}

func (apiHandler) ServeHTTP(http.ResponseWriter, *http.Request) {}

func main() {
	mux := http.NewServeMux()
	mux.Handle("/api/", apiHandler{})
	mux.HandleFunc("/", func(w http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request) {
		// The "/" pattern matches everything, so we need to check
		// that we're at the root here.
		if req.URL.Path != "/" {
			http.NotFound(w, req)
			return
		}
		fmt.Fprintf(w, "Welcome to the home page!")
	})
}


********************************************************************

</pre>  --  



********************************************************************

<pre>  --  Output:

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  


********************************************************************

</p>  --

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="ServeMux.Handler" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=2436">  --  Handler

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#ServeMux.Handler">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (mux *

********************************************************************

<a href="#ServeMux">  --  ServeMux

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) Handler(r *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) (h 

********************************************************************

<a href="#Handler">  --  Handler

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , pattern 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  Handler returns the handler to use for the given request,
consulting r.Method, r.Host, and r.URL.Path. It always returns
a non-nil handler. If the path is not in its canonical form, the
handler will be an internally-generated handler that redirects
to the canonical path. If the host contains a port, it is ignored
when matching handlers.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  The path and host are used unchanged for CONNECT requests.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Handler also returns the registered pattern that matches the
request or, in the case of internally-generated redirects,
the pattern that will match after following the redirect.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  If there is no registered handler that applies to the request,
Handler returns a “page not found” handler and an empty pattern.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Server.Close" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=2722">  --  Close

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Server.Close">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (srv *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Server">  --  Server

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) Close() 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  Close immediately closes all active net.Listeners and any
connections in state StateNew, StateActive, or StateIdle. For a
graceful shutdown, use Shutdown.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Close does not attempt to close (and does not even know about)
any hijacked connections, such as WebSockets.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Close returns any error returned from closing the Server's
underlying Listener(s).


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Server.ListenAndServe" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=2976">  --  ListenAndServe

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Server.ListenAndServe">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (srv *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Server">  --  Server

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) ListenAndServe() 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  ListenAndServe listens on the TCP network address srv.Addr and then
calls Serve to handle requests on incoming connections.
Accepted connections are configured to enable TCP keep-alives.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  If srv.Addr is blank, ":http" is used.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  ListenAndServe always returns a non-nil error. After Shutdown or Close,
the returned error is ErrServerClosed.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Server.ListenAndServeTLS" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=3270">  --  ListenAndServeTLS

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Server.ListenAndServeTLS">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (srv *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Server">  --  Server

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) ListenAndServeTLS(certFile, keyFile 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  ListenAndServeTLS listens on the TCP network address srv.Addr and
then calls ServeTLS to handle requests on incoming TLS connections.
Accepted connections are configured to enable TCP keep-alives.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Filenames containing a certificate and matching private key for the
server must be provided if neither the Server's TLSConfig.Certificates
nor TLSConfig.GetCertificate are populated. If the certificate is
signed by a certificate authority, the certFile should be the
concatenation of the server's certificate, any intermediates, and
the CA's certificate.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  If srv.Addr is blank, ":https" is used.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  ListenAndServeTLS always returns a non-nil error. After Shutdown or
Close, the returned error is ErrServerClosed.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Server.RegisterOnShutdown" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=2815">  --  RegisterOnShutdown

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Server.RegisterOnShutdown">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (srv *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Server">  --  Server

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) RegisterOnShutdown(f func())

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  RegisterOnShutdown registers a function to call on Shutdown.
This can be used to gracefully shutdown connections that have
undergone ALPN protocol upgrade or that have been hijacked.
This function should start protocol-specific graceful shutdown,
but should not wait for shutdown to complete.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Server.Serve" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=3029">  --  Serve

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Server.Serve">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (srv *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Server">  --  Server

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) Serve(l 

********************************************************************

<a href="/net?GOOS=linux">  --  net

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/net?GOOS=linux#Listener">  --  Listener

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  Serve accepts incoming connections on the Listener l, creating a
new service goroutine for each. The service goroutines read requests and
then call srv.Handler to reply to them.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  HTTP/2 support is only enabled if the Listener returns *tls.Conn
connections and they were configured with "h2" in the TLS
Config.NextProtos.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Serve always returns a non-nil error and closes l.
After Shutdown or Close, the returned error is ErrServerClosed.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Server.ServeTLS" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=3106">  --  ServeTLS

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Server.ServeTLS">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (srv *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Server">  --  Server

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) ServeTLS(l 

********************************************************************

<a href="/net?GOOS=linux">  --  net

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/net?GOOS=linux#Listener">  --  Listener

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , certFile, keyFile 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  ServeTLS accepts incoming connections on the Listener l, creating a
new service goroutine for each. The service goroutines perform TLS
setup and then read requests, calling srv.Handler to reply to them.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Files containing a certificate and matching private key for the
server must be provided if neither the Server's
TLSConfig.Certificates nor TLSConfig.GetCertificate are populated.
If the certificate is signed by a certificate authority, the
certFile should be the concatenation of the server's certificate,
any intermediates, and the CA's certificate.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  ServeTLS always returns a non-nil error. After Shutdown or Close, the
returned error is ErrServerClosed.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Server.SetKeepAlivesEnabled" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=3200">  --  SetKeepAlivesEnabled

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Server.SetKeepAlivesEnabled">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (srv *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Server">  --  Server

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) SetKeepAlivesEnabled(v 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#bool">  --  bool

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  SetKeepAlivesEnabled controls whether HTTP keep-alives are enabled.
By default, keep-alives are always enabled. Only very
resource-constrained environments or servers in the process of
shutting down should disable them.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Server.Shutdown" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/server.go;l=2772">  --  Shutdown

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Server.Shutdown">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (srv *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Server">  --  Server

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) Shutdown(ctx 

********************************************************************

<a href="/context?GOOS=linux">  --  context

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/context?GOOS=linux#Context">  --  Context

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  Shutdown gracefully shuts down the server without interrupting any
active connections. Shutdown works by first closing all open
listeners, then closing all idle connections, and then waiting
indefinitely for connections to return to idle and then shut down.
If the provided context expires before the shutdown is complete,
Shutdown returns the context's error, otherwise it returns any
error returned from closing the Server's underlying Listener(s).


********************************************************************

<p>  --  When Shutdown is called, Serve, ListenAndServe, and
ListenAndServeTLS immediately return ErrServerClosed. Make sure the
program doesn't exit and waits instead for Shutdown to return.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Shutdown does not attempt to close nor wait for hijacked
connections such as WebSockets. The caller of Shutdown should
separately notify such long-lived connections of shutdown and wait
for them to close, if desired. See RegisterOnShutdown for a way to
register shutdown notification functions.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Once Shutdown has been called on a server, it may not be reused;
future calls to methods such as Serve will return ErrServerClosed.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  


********************************************************************

<a href="#example-Server.Shutdown">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  


********************************************************************

<pre class="Documentation-exampleCode">  --  
package main

import (
	"context"
	"log"
	"net/http"
	"os"
	"os/signal"
)

func main() {
	var srv http.Server

	idleConnsClosed := make(chan struct{})
	go func() {
		sigint := make(chan os.Signal, 1)
		signal.Notify(sigint, os.Interrupt)
		<-sigint

		// We received an interrupt signal, shut down.
		if err := srv.Shutdown(context.Background()); err != nil {
			// Error from closing listeners, or context timeout:
			log.Printf("HTTP server Shutdown: %v", err)
		}
		close(idleConnsClosed)
	}()

	if err := srv.ListenAndServe(); err != http.ErrServerClosed {
		// Error starting or closing listener:
		log.Fatalf("HTTP server ListenAndServe: %v", err)
	}

	<-idleConnsClosed
}


********************************************************************

</pre>  --  



********************************************************************

<pre>  --  Output:

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  


********************************************************************

</p>  --  
        

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Transport" data-kind="type" class="Documentation-typeHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/transport.go;l=95">  --  Transport

<pre>  --  type Transport struct {



********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) (*

********************************************************************

<a href="/net/url?GOOS=linux">  --  url

</a>  --  ,

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )



********************************************************************

<a href="/context?GOOS=linux">  --  context

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/context?GOOS=linux#Context">  --  Context

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , proxyURL *

********************************************************************

<a href="/net/url?GOOS=linux">  --  url

********************************************************************

</a>  --  .

********************************************************************

<a href="/net/url?GOOS=linux#URL">  --  URL

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , connectReq *

<a href="/net/url?GOOS=linux#URL">  --  URL
