</a>  --  , target 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) (

********************************************************************

<a href="#Header">  --  Header

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )



********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#int64">  --  int64

********************************************************************

</a>  --  



********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#int">  --  int

********************************************************************

</a>  --  



********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#int">  --  int

********************************************************************

</a>  --  



********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#bool">  --  bool

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
	

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  Transport is an implementation of RoundTripper that supports HTTP,
HTTPS, and HTTP proxies (for either HTTP or HTTPS with CONNECT).


********************************************************************

<p>  --  By default, Transport caches connections for future re-use.
This may leave many open connections when accessing many hosts.
This behavior can be managed using Transport's CloseIdleConnections method
and the MaxIdleConnsPerHost and DisableKeepAlives fields.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Transports should be reused instead of created as needed.
Transports are safe for concurrent use by multiple goroutines.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  A Transport is a low-level primitive for making HTTP and HTTPS requests.
For high-level functionality, such as cookies and redirects, see Client.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Transport uses HTTP/1.1 for HTTP URLs and either HTTP/1.1 or HTTP/2
for HTTPS URLs, depending on whether the server supports HTTP/2,
and how the Transport is configured. The DefaultTransport supports HTTP/2.
To explicitly enable HTTP/2 on a transport, use golang.org/x/net/http2
and call ConfigureTransport. See the package docs for more about HTTP/2.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Responses with status codes in the 1xx range are either handled
automatically (100 expect-continue) or ignored. The one
exception is HTTP status code 101 (Switching Protocols), which is
considered a terminal status and returned by RoundTrip. To see the
ignored 1xx responses, use the httptrace trace package's
ClientTrace.Got1xxResponse.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Transport only retries a request upon encountering a network error
if the request is idempotent and either has no body or has its
Request.GetBody defined. HTTP requests are considered idempotent if
they have HTTP methods GET, HEAD, OPTIONS, or TRACE; or if their
Header map contains an "Idempotency-Key" or "X-Idempotency-Key"
entry. If the idempotency key value is a zero-length slice, the
request is treated as idempotent but the header is not sent on the
wire.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  


********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Transport.CancelRequest" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
          

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/transport.go;l=796">  --  CancelRequest

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
            

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

      

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (t *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Transport">  --  Transport

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) CancelRequest(req *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  CancelRequest cancels an in-flight request by closing its connection.
CancelRequest should only be called after RoundTrip has returned.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Deprecated: Use Request.WithContext to create a request with a
cancelable context instead. CancelRequest cannot cancel HTTP/2
requests.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

      

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Transport.CloseIdleConnections" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/transport.go;l=772">  --  CloseIdleConnections

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Transport.CloseIdleConnections">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (t *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Transport">  --  Transport

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) CloseIdleConnections()

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  CloseIdleConnections closes any connections which were previously
connected from previous requests but are now sitting idle in
a "keep-alive" state. It does not interrupt any connections currently
in use.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Transport.RegisterProtocol" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/transport.go;l=753">  --  RegisterProtocol

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Transport.RegisterProtocol">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (t *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Transport">  --  Transport

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) RegisterProtocol(scheme 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#string">  --  string

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , rt 

********************************************************************

<a href="#RoundTripper">  --  RoundTripper

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  RegisterProtocol registers a new protocol with scheme.
The Transport will pass requests using the given scheme to rt.
It is rt's responsibility to simulate HTTP request semantics.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  RegisterProtocol can be used by other packages to provide
implementations of protocol schemes like "ftp" or "file".


********************************************************************

<p>  --  If rt.RoundTrip returns ErrSkipAltProtocol, the Transport will
handle the RoundTrip itself for that one request, as if the
protocol were not registered.


********************************************************************

</p>  --  

  

  

********************************************************************

<h4 tabindex="-1" id="Transport.RoundTrip" data-kind="method" class="Documentation-typeMethodHeader">  --  
      

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-source" href="https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.20.7:src/net/http/roundtrip.go;l=16">  --  RoundTrip

********************************************************************

</a>  --   

********************************************************************

<a class="Documentation-idLink" href="#Transport.RoundTrip">  --  ¶

********************************************************************

</a>  --  
  

********************************************************************

</h4>  --  

    
    

********************************************************************

<pre>  --  func (t *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Transport">  --  Transport

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) RoundTrip(req *

********************************************************************

<a href="#Request">  --  Request

********************************************************************

</a>  --  ) (*

********************************************************************

<a href="#Response">  --  Response

********************************************************************

</a>  --  , 

********************************************************************

<a href="/builtin?GOOS=linux#error">  --  error

********************************************************************

</a>  --  )

********************************************************************

</pre>  --  
    

********************************************************************

<p>  --  RoundTrip implements the RoundTripper interface.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  For higher-level HTTP client support (such as handling of cookies
and redirects), see Get, Post, and the Client type.


********************************************************************

<p>  --  Like the RoundTripper interface, the error types returned
by RoundTrip are unspecified.


********************************************************************

</p>  --
